<Time>1601741973035</Time><Response>None<//Response>< text>
I  tried to give this establishment a few tries. You can never go wrong with BR ice cream. Employees that are here are hit or miss. Last night was the final straw for me. Read below for situation.

BR closes at 10:00 on a Friday night, went to get my car wash and grab some ice cream. Walked in at 9:48/9:49 but they had things covering the ice cream. I asked if they were already closed and they said "no, you can still get ice cream". There were 3 employees there, 2 of which were not wearing gloves, the other having cash out on the counter. I waited for about 5 minutes with no help, literally just standing there. At 9:56, one of the employees told me that they were already closed and that in the future... I cut him off and had to tell him I asked if they were closed before I waited and that I've been waiting for one of them to help me. The other employee told me "well that was a few minutes ago and we're closed now", which I then tried to explain one of them could've helped me get the ice cream and not have to wait. They tried to back out of their previous statement and that I could order, but that they were already closed due to their computer system clock. I decided not to order anything, and go to another ice cream shop in TO.

I feel that this establishment has incompetent employees as to what to do with regards to customer satisfaction. This is the worst experience out of the half dozen times I've been there. Not very many times to go here and to continuously have problems with their employees.< /text>

<Rate>3<//Rate><text>I was in Clovis a couple of weeks ago from Atlanta to be with my 80 year old elderly mother who just got diagnosed with cancer.  She  lives in Clovis on her own. On the last day I was there, I noticed the temperature of her house was at 60 and her thermostat was set at 72 -- blowing cold air.  When I got back to Atlanta, I googled HVAC companies. Controlled Climates had good reviews, so I called them to see if they could go to my moms home and check what the problem was and possibly fix it.  They were very nice but told me that the earliest available time they had to go to my moms was I think the 2nd week of Dec. I told them my moms age and that she is sick and needed more immediate attention so I would look elsewhere. They told me they could possibly bump it up to the week of Thanksgiving.  I told them that was not good enough and I would have to look elsewhere. They then told me to hold on and that they would call me back. When they called back, they could miraculously  be there in 1/2 hour.  How nice I thought.  How lucky I got...I thought.

They arrived at the time they said.  I called my mom and told her to have them call me as soon as they were finished diagnosing the problem.  I spoke with the technician after he was through, and I was informed that unfortunately the furnace had all sorts of issues and was going to be over $1000.00 to fix. I was told that realistically everything was in such bad shape, it wasn't worth the fix. He recommended a brand new furnace with an air purifier -- a total estimate bill of $4,400.00!  Needless to say, I was extremely disappointed over this news. Because of the cost, I declined their immediate services, and opted to get a second opinion.

The next day, I found another HVAC company to come in and check out the problem. They were in and out in less than 45 minutes. They told me it was a loose 24v cable to the gas valve causing the problem and saw no other issues.  They fixed it for $85.00, and my mom had heat.  I brought up the problems that Controlled Climates had mentioned to me, and I was told that if they saw anything like that they also would have brought it to my attention, but they didn't.

I'm not accusing Controlled Climates of any wrongdoing.  I'm just stating facts. They say they have pictures and insist they did everything on the up and up. They defend themselves very well. I however, inconveniently live 2500 miles away. And they knew that. What can I do at this distance except question something that sounds pretty extreme. My mom is elderly and very trusting.  I however, not so much. I'm glad that I called someone else. A week and a half later, and with a savings of $4,315.00, my moms furnace is humming along just fine after a thorough inspection and fix by another company.

You be the judge.

Update 12/2/2018

I received a very professional phone call from the owner Mr. Ray Montez.  After reading my review he expressed how sorry he was and didn't like knowing that I felt that way about him or his company. He told me that sometimes one technician can spend 1 hour trying to fix something (which is what he did) and not be able to fix or find the problem and another can come in and get lucky.  It can happen.

I was really satisfied with his attempt to repair his image with me more than his concern about his review online.  That is what I really respected about his phone call. He didn't tell me to take down my review.  He came across as courteous, professional, ethical and honestly sorry about not being able to find the problem.  He offered to refund my money and provide some maintenance services for free.  I declined.

I really appreciated his phone call and wish him and his company well.<//text><pics>None</pics><Resp>{'time': 1551733560465, 'text': 'Thank you for your feedback J W. From the start the operater was very polite and explained my options. We ended up doing the annual maintenance plan. The repair man came out a few days later. I was texted to know he was on the way. He did a thorough job checking out the AC unit. He showed a new part was needed and then took the time to show us on the manual of how the unit was not performing correctly. Then he tested it again and showed the unit was back in properly functioning parameters with the new part installed. He then re insulated the cabling and caulked and sealed them to prevent insects and moisture from getting in our househ He then went on his way. The process took most of the two hour window that we had scheduled.

I was very happy on how thorough he was on the unit. I also appreciated him taking the time to explain to me why I needed the part instead of a "just trust me" attitude. I learned some new things. I highly recommend this company for your servicing needs.< /text>

I asked the barber to use scissors on the side instead of clippers and his response was that he couldn't because he might cut my ears.
Let that sink in.
This guy has been cutting hair for at least 30 years and he doesn't know how to use scissors? Ironically, he finished the haircut with a straight razor...around my ears!
